<Review>01-05-2018
Not enough signage to really help the driver know what lane to be in. (Left lane to scale coming in).
Gate people disinterested in truck drivers was my feeling. Check-in window at docks the gal was helpful.
Scale at the docks is registers under weight my guess is about 500 pounds.
When I told security, the man at the exit gate seemed angry when i reported my tandem axles were at 34200.
Not too much but my steers showed 11100.
That's when the flags in my brain went up. My girl tanks were almost full and the steers generally weigh in at 11700.
This is a legacy operation akin to Safeway or Del Monte or the old businesses that have been around so long they cannot operate efficiently like say Costco DC and some of the newer places that do not hold the driver up 5 6 or seven hours for a twenty minute job.
(Big sigh)
They took one pallet off the back, I'm all better now.
Still, 5 hours to load...
Just saying.</Review></record></dataset><record>

1 taco de carne asada

< Text>
Qimura is new sushi restaurant in Windsor, it is in the same location as the closed Senju restaurant. We tried it after we received a flier advertising the change in ownership, and we weren't disappointed.
We sampled multiple nigiri, including sake, hamachi and unagi, plus had the sashimi plate that included maguro. The sushi was first class and very well prepared.

We returned to Qimura today, and while the sushi is still very good, the service was extremely slow. We counted 8 staff all hanging around trying to look busy, but waited about 40 minutes for our first roll to be served. I don't think this place will survive unless they figure out how to speed up the sushi making.< /Text>

<text>After 7 or 8 years of visiting various shooting ranges, I will say this is the indoor shooting range in which I feel the safest seeing as to how they ask every nonmember to demonstrate their firearms safety conduct. If you fail the safety demonstration, they will politely but firmly ask you to leave (so you don't end up endangering other shooters). Before visiting this range, be sure to fully understand and fully obey:
1) The firearms safety rules as outlined by Jeff Cooper
2) The range rules for The Firing Line found on their website
3) How to safely operate any firearm you plan on renting from or bringing to the range

Additionally, their annual membership is reasonably priced and pays off after 9 visits, or 7 visits if you rent one handgun per visit. The range itself is in a good, reasonably accessible location for people living in Los Angeles County, Pasadena, and far east as Rosemead.

Parking: They have 7-9 parking spots in a lot behind the shooting range. There is also street parking very close to the range. Parking was never an issue for me for all of my visits. This shooting range is more busy on the weekends, like most businesses and establishments.

I will end on what I feel is the most important note and I wish there was a way I could emphasize this more but: I am consistently blown away by the professionalism and friendliness of all staff members with each range visit on any given day of the week. This is one of the few ranges where I feel genuinely welcome.</text>< UserId.>

< text>
Location:
Great location with parking space in the back (about 13 total)

Safety:
.There are no range officer inside the two shooting areas
.There are a lots of beginner leading to a lots of gun miss handling (such as not pointing the guns in the safest direction and not reloading guns in the booth)

Staff:
Customer service is overall mediocre because of their cocky attitudes (stay away from Todd)
Anytime you need help it look like you are annoying them

Ammunition:
You can not bring your own ammunition (except for .22lr)
Their reload ammunitions are really dirty
The ammunition is expensive

Gun:
Good selection of the most commun guns on the market.
Gun are no very well clean which leads to jam from time to time.
No shotgun allowed and no rapid fire</text>

(Translated by Google) The worst shooting range in Los Angeles and surely in the whole of the United States. I shoot in most of the US states but I have never been so disappointed. Firstly no information on the prices, there were 2 of us but can only have one weapon and one line so each take turns, in other words no one. A really poor choice of handgun and even worse semi automatic rifle. The prices are staggering 98 dollars for 2 handguns (a 9mm and a .45) 50 rounds of each or in other shooting ranges it is about 10 dollars the rental of the weapon plus 14-18 dollars for the 50 cartridges. Avoid this establishment if you are not a member and instead direct you towards more "tourist" ranges like the "los angeles shooting club." Highlight of the show he forgets to give us our 2 IDs so let's turn around 25 km to Pick them up. The only good thing is the parking lot. You know every good stay in Los Angeles.

<Review>I was in the market for a new mattress and came across Mattress Firm Richmond using Google. Mattress Firm offered financing with 0% interest using their Mattress Firm credit card through Synchrony Bank. As far as I could tell, they were the only mattress retailer that had any special financing deals, but their prices were pretty reasonable too. Applying was easy and quick online and got the approval within seconds. If you have no credit or bad credit you could also get financing through Progressive Leasing. The rates are probably higher and doubt they have 0% interest specials, but at least you can finance your purchase.

I called Mattress Firm Richmond to see if they were open and they were. I spoke to Diane and she mentioned that they were open but by appointment only. Diane was extremely helpful and informative. She not only squeezed me into an appointment for the next day but also took a few minutes to listen to what I was looking for and provide me with a little bit of information. Obviously I would get more 1-on-1 service during my appointment but it didn't stop her from taking the time to share her knowledge and expertise with me.

At my appointment, Connie helped me and my wife pick out the right mattress for us. Connie mentioned she was from another store but I'm glad she was there during our appointment. She had us try a few different types of mattresses first to get a feel for the difference in comfort. Our mattress of only 2.5 years old felt like it wasn't supportive enough so we thought we needed a firm mattress. Connie took the time to explain to us the difference between a firm mattress and a mattress with firm support.

Long story short, we settled on a Serta mattress that had firm support and some cushioning. The mattress with a little more cushioning felt more comfortable but we opted to save about $400 so we could get an adjustable base. Note that you can get a free adjustable base with a purchase of $699 and up but it's their basic model. We opted to pay a little more for the Serta adjustable base because it was more quiet and smooth when operating. We've never had an adjustable base so my wife and I are excited to receive our new mattress.

Fortunately, the mattress we selected was in their warehouse so we're getting our mattress within 24 hours. We did purchase during their Memorial Day sale, which is the biggest sale of the year for them aside from Labor Day so I can't guarantee that they'll have the same sales and discounts on their bases, delivery fees or extended warranties. We saved over $1000 and couldn't be happier with our purchase.

Hopefully the mattress works out for us for the next 10 years but we'd definitely look no further than Mattress Firm Richmond for our future mattress needs. Based on my experience, I'd highly recommend them.

Updated 5/20/2020: My mattress wasn't delivered the next day as expected because it wasn't actually in stock even though it showed up as 1. I called the store back and spoke to Connie again. She apologized for the delay but told me that it was expected to be back in stock on Wednesday so I should get it by Thursday. I was a little disappointed but happy to hear that I wouldn't have to wait too much longer to receive the bed. I didn't receive a call to inform me of the delivery for tomorrow but I'm hopeful it will. < Text>
We went one of the first two opening days.  The place was packed within 20 minutes of sitting down. Thank goodness for the owner coming around to tables because the server we had was not selling us on any of their options. No recommendations and couldn't tell us about the flavor/ different heat levels on the chicken except the names and order of heat:
1) skerd 2) dang 3) redneckulous
Don't be afraid of the heat. If you like flavor with a kick go with the middle option. It's not spicy like you'd think.
The onion rings were delicious.
We ordered a chicken sandwich (skerd)
and a chicken meal with two sides (dang)
The sandwich was dry, it needed something and I wish I would have went spicier.
The chicken meal was good, side of mac and cheese, great!
Nice variety of beers on tap although, no N.A. option, which would be great if that happens!
Seeing how we went opening week, we'll likely give it some time to iron out the rough edges and visit again.
We enjoyed the baseball game on while we ate, chatting with the owner for a moment, and the quick service.<//Text>

< text>
Came here for lunch with my friend.  He got the western burger with tots... while I wasn't that hungry so I ordered of the happy hour menu... sliders with fries. Note happy hour is every day from 3pm-6pm. We also shared an order of the bun street tots.

The burger looked impressive and appetizing.   There was a lot going.... bacon, bbq sauce, onion rings, melty cheese, lettuce, pickle and tomato. The meat was good, the onion rings where nice and crispy. The bbq sauce was a bit on the sweet side.  I think it would have been better with a bbq that had more of a smoky flavor.  Also I don't typically see western burgers with the veggies.

The bun street tots consisted of grilled onions with boys of bacon and there version of 1,000 island sauce. I thought the fries were just ok.  The sauce was fine but missing something. And the grilled onions with bacon were just slightly on the salty side.

The sliders were simple meat bread burgers.... nothing to write hone about.  But I will say they did have the brioche bun just right.  Moist and fluffy! Very yummy.

The service was average.... friendly.</text>

<Text>Favorite Burger Joint in West Co.
Outstanding burger quality, delicious sides, and fantastic beer selection.

This review is LONG over due. I've been coming to this place for years. The burger quality will have you craving for more once you've had it.

The prepared burgers are delicious, and they offer a build your own, if you're undecided. Good selection of sides. The tots are delicious.

The beer selection is great too. Pairs well with the tastiness of their food.

Atmosphere is modern, and clean. The staff is always amazing. Best of all, they are dog friendly. I've brought my little fur buddy to seat with me at their patio section. The staff always offers waters and bowls. That really means a lot.

As I've said, this is my favorite burger joint in town. High praise for this place.</Text><Pics>None< /Pics>< resp>

<user_id>104582250582946827448< /user_id><Name>Dale Sandler<//Name><Date>1563485604102</Date>< rate>
5< /rate>
< text>
I tried this place yesterday based on reviews on Google. There were a couple of small issues: The server couldn't answer in anything other than a commercial. "What is in the bun sauce?" "It's a house version based on Thousand Island dressing. It's very good!" A little irritating as I only wanted an answer not an advert. Additionally the meat was cooked a little differently than I expected. This is understandable as there is no universal measure for rare, medium or well. There is always a little variation and I would recommend that you ask for your burger to be cooked a little more than you normally have it as they tend to undercook a little - my medium was closer to what I would consider medium rare as was my daughter-in-law's, my wife's well was closer to what she considered medium-well.
Other than those small issues, this place is amazing! The house sauce is very good, the burgers were very tasty and generous in size, the onion rings were decent and the fries were so good, I would go back just for those alone. All in all a very good experience.<//text>

<Text>I had never had Peruvian food and decided to give this place a try after having passed it many times. Checked it out on TA, found very favorable reviews, and off I went on a Thursday evening. It was close to 7:00pm on a weekenight, but 3/4 filled with people enjoying themselves. It is not fancy inside, nor is it plain. The ambience is casual and very friendly. The menu has plenty of choices and many of the dishes come in your choice of fish, chicken or beef. I had a shredded chicken in a delicious sauce over wonderful potatoes...and big mound of very flavorful rice on the side. Yup, potatoes and rice. As many other TA reviewers have noted, it works! The portion was fine; some of the other dishes had very large portions. Bottom line, do not be afraid to try this cuisine if it is new to you. The dishes are like good comfort food, nothing that should in any way scare off a timid palate. You will like it. Everyone I talk to who has gone, does. And the prices are terrific.< /Text><UserId.>107065486287042954197<//UserId.><Date>1561186746773</Date><rate>5</rate>< response>

We were just down the street and hungry. Google Maps listed this place and it was new to us so we stopped. Glad we did. We got the Homemade onion rings and Mozzarella sticks for appetizers. Rings were light and crispy with a slight Teriyaki zip to them. Excellent. The Mozzarella sticks were just OK. I thought the California burger was very good. The Stinkin' Bun Burger was voted good too. The burgers don't come with fries so I ordered the Seasoned fries which, curiously aren't seasoned. At All. Just plain fries. Maybe a hint of salt but not what you'd expect. They are good as plain old fries tho. We also ordered a Chicken Salad but I didn't get any as she wouldn't share so I can't comment. LOL. Chocolate chip cookie served warm with Vanilla Icecream on top with chocolate drizzle was delicious.< /Text>

< Review>
The first time we found this place was when my wife and I were at Ikea and were looking for a local place to eat. We tried this place and loved it. They make delicious burger creations and tasty parmesan garlic fries.

We like this place so much that we constantly ask each other if we need anything from Ikea just so we can stop at Bun Street. We've had just about all of their signature burgers and they are all very good that I can't decide which is my favorite. Maybe it's  the California Burger.

Decent burgers joint, nice suggested combinations and good üçü fries. They have a a variety of bun options but a "gluten free bun*" was  not an option unfortunately. But they gladly lettuce rapped my California Burger. Which along with the service was very nice... To sum up the place, this restaurant is a inspiring burger joint with the price tag to match. They have interesting customization options to choose from throughout their menu. david adams<//Name>
<review>Bun Street is a burger place. They serve specialty burgers, salads, sides, craft fries, tots, soft drinks, wine, and beer. You also have an option of building your own burger.

We were greeted upon entry and asked if we wanted to sit outside or inside. We requested for indoor seating. They sat us on the third table from the far right. It was nice that they gave us space from the other tables. Another server came by and asked if we wanted anything to drink. Within a few minutes, she took our orders.

I ordered the Mac N' Cheese Burger. It was fantastic! Huge portion of the mac and cheese. The mac and cheese portion was superb. Rich cheese flavor and the macaroni texture was soft with a slight firmness to it. The angus beef patty was thick and juicy. The BBQ sauce was sweet and not overly heavy. The lettuce was fresh. The buns were soft and held the burger together nicely. At no point did the buns become soggy. I didn't think mac and cheese would work on a burger but surprisingly it did. This had to be one of the best burgers I've had. Since we arrived before 3pm on a weekday, the burger came with a side of fries. The fries were perfect. They were crispy on the outside and soft in the middle.

The Pizza Fries were pretty good. The fries portion was huge. The pepperoni was slightly spicy, the marinara was zesty, and the mozzarella was milky. I ended up eating the rest of the fries when we got home. It was much better then because by that point the marinara was fully absorbed into the fries making it very rich and packed with flavor.

The service was great. The food arrived within 15 minutes. Our server was very friendly and incredibly attentive. When we folded up the straw paper and left it on the table, she came by randomly and picked it up. After we had a few bites of our food, she came by and asked how everything was. When she saw that I was fumbling for napkins, she asked if I wanted more napkins. After we put everything in boxes, she asked if she could take the plates out of he way. It wasn't like she was standing next to us the whole time. It just seemed like the timing was perfect when she came out to ask things.

Indoor seating consists of a long wooden booth with tables and metal chairs on the opposite side. These tables were in close proximity with each other. There is also bar seating. There are lots of TVs on the walls and they were all on mute.

The Mac N' Cheese Burger was fantastic and the Pizza Fries were pretty good. I did get massive heartburn afterwords but it was worth it. I'll be back for another visit.< /review><user_id>114085413776062826851</user_id>< gmapID>
0x80c3282bd02cb517:0xfe8dd417237fd42b</gmapID>

ORIGINAL REVIEW
